## חֹב (id: 002073000000000)

חֹב
===

חֹב (H2243)

noun m · חבב

Clothing

fold (of garment) \= small bag formed by a folded piece of cloth; ◄ part a garment; ► used to carry small objects, ≈ which will not be visible from the outside and therefore associated with secrecy

[JOB 31:33](https://ref.ly/Job31:33)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 31:33


## חבא (id: 002074000000000)

חבא
===

חבא (H2244)

verb · אֶלְיַחְבָּא

Solid

to freeze \= process by which liquids become solid, ◄ caused by low temperatures during cold weather

[JOB 38:30](https://ref.ly/Job38:30)

verb · חבה · מַחֲבֵא · מַחֲבֹוא · אֶלְיַחְבָּא

Hide

to hide oneself \= action by which humans go to a location where they will not be readily seen by others; ► in order to be safe from danger or to attack someone else

[GEN 3:8](https://ref.ly/Gen3:8) · [GEN 3:10](https://ref.ly/Gen3:10) · [JOS 2:16](https://ref.ly/Josh2:16) · [JOS 10:16](https://ref.ly/Josh10:16) · [JOS 10:17](https://ref.ly/Josh10:17) · [JOS 10:27](https://ref.ly/Josh10:27) · [JDG 9:5](https://ref.ly/Judg9:5) · [1SA 10:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:22) · [1SA 13:6](https://ref.ly/1Sam13:6) · [1SA 14:11](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:11) · [1SA 14:22](https://ref.ly/1Sam14:22) · [1SA 19:2](https://ref.ly/1Sam19:2) · [1SA 23:23](https://ref.ly/1Sam23:23) · [2SA 17:9](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:9) · [2KI 11:3](https://ref.ly/2Kgs11:3) · [1CH 21:20](https://ref.ly/1Chr21:20) · [2CH 18:24](https://ref.ly/2Chr18:24) · [2CH 22:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr22:9) · [2CH 22:12](https://ref.ly/2Chr22:12) · [JOB 24:4](https://ref.ly/Job24:4) · [JOB 29:8](https://ref.ly/Job29:8) · [DAN 10:7](https://ref.ly/Dan10:7) · [AMO 9:3](https://ref.ly/Amos9:3)

Hide

to hide (someone) \= causative action by which humans cause someone else to go to a location where that person will not be readily seen by others, ► in order to keep that person out of danger or to remove him/her from public life

[JOS 6:17](https://ref.ly/Josh6:17) · [JOS 6:25](https://ref.ly/Josh6:25) · [1KI 18:4](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:4) · [1KI 18:13](https://ref.ly/1Kgs18:13) · [2KI 6:29](https://ref.ly/2Kgs6:29) · [ISA 42:22](https://ref.ly/Isa42:22)

Non\-Know

to act in secret \= action by which humans act in a such a way that other people do not notice

[GEN 31:27](https://ref.ly/Gen31:27)

Safe

to hide, to protect \= causative action by which someone keep someone else from (physical or non\-physical) harm

[JOB 5:21](https://ref.ly/Job5:21) · [ISA 49:2](https://ref.ly/Isa49:2)

Non\-Speak

**Collocation:** קֹול חבא

(one's) voice hides \> to refrain from speaking literally: to hide oneself (of one's voice); hence: \= action by which humans refrain from speaking

[JOB 29:10](https://ref.ly/Job29:10)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 38:30; Genesis 3:8; Genesis 3:10; Joshua 2:16; Joshua 10:16; Joshua 10:17; Joshua 10:27; Judges 9:5; 1 Samuel 10:22; 1 Samuel 13:6; 1 Samuel 14:11; 1 Samuel 14:22; 1 Samuel 19:2; 1 Samuel 23:23; 2 Samuel 17:9; 2 Kings 11:3; 1 Chronicles 21:20; 2 Chronicles 18:24; 2 Chronicles 22:9; 2 Chronicles 22:12; Job 24:4; Job 29:8; Daniel 10:7; Amos 9:3; Joshua 6:17; Joshua 6:25; 1 Kings 18:4; 1 Kings 18:13; 2 Kings 6:29; Isaiah 42:22; Genesis 31:27; Job 5:21; Isaiah 49:2; Job 29:10

## חַבּוּרָה (id: 002081000000000)

חַבּוּרָה

חַבּוּרָה (H2250)

noun f · חֲבַרְבֻּרֹות

Impact

wound, bruise \= area of physical damage on the body; ◄ caused by sickness or aggression; ≈ sometimes used in a figurative sense to refer to difficult circumstances

[GEN 4:23](https://ref.ly/Gen4:23) · [EXO 21:25](https://ref.ly/Exod21:25) · [EXO 21:25](https://ref.ly/Exod21:25) · [PSA 38:6](https://ref.ly/Ps38:6) · [PRO 20:30](https://ref.ly/Prov20:30) · [ISA 1:6](https://ref.ly/Isa1:6) · [ISA 53:5](https://ref.ly/Isa53:5)

## חבל (id: 002085000000000)

חבל
===

חבל (H2254a · H2254b · H2254c · A2255)

verb · חֲבֹל · חֶבֶל · חֲבֹלָה

Non\-Possess

to take as pledge \= causative action by which humans seize an object as a pledge for a loan

[EXO 22:25](https://ref.ly/Exod22:25) · [EXO 22:25](https://ref.ly/Exod22:25) · [DEU 24:6](https://ref.ly/Deut24:6) · [DEU 24:6](https://ref.ly/Deut24:6) · [DEU 24:17](https://ref.ly/Deut24:17) · [JOB 22:6](https://ref.ly/Job22:6) · [JOB 24:3](https://ref.ly/Job24:3) · [JOB 24:9](https://ref.ly/Job24:9)2 · [PRO 20:16](https://ref.ly/Prov20:16) · [PRO 27:13](https://ref.ly/Prov27:13) · [EZK 18:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek18:16) · [AMO 2:8](https://ref.ly/Amos2:8)

verb · חֶבֶל · חֲבָל · חֲבוּלָה

Impact

to destroy, to ruin, to devastate, to break, to harm \= causative action by which someone brings destruction and suffering upon humans and inanimate objects

[EZR 6:12](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:12) · [PRO 13:13](https://ref.ly/Prov13:13) · [ECC 5:5](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:5) · [SNG 2:15](https://ref.ly/Song2:15) · [ISA 13:5](https://ref.ly/Isa13:5) · [ISA 32:7](https://ref.ly/Isa32:7) · [ISA 54:16](https://ref.ly/Isa54:16) · [DAN 4:20](https://ref.ly/Dan4:20) · [DAN 6:23](https://ref.ly/Dan6:23) · [MIC 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mic2:10)1

End

to break \> to bring to an end literally: to break an event; hence: \= causative action by which someone brings an event to an end

[JOB 17:1](https://ref.ly/Job17:1)3 · [ISA 10:27](https://ref.ly/Isa10:27) · [DAN 2:44](https://ref.ly/Dan2:44) · [DAN 6:27](https://ref.ly/Dan6:27) · [DAN 7:14](https://ref.ly/Dan7:14)

Sin

to act wickedly \= action by which humans act in a morally and ethically unacceptable way

[NEH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Neh1:7) · [NEH 1:7](https://ref.ly/Neh1:7) · [JOB 34:31](https://ref.ly/Job34:31)

verb · חֵבֶל

Birth

to give birth \= action by which living creatures give birth; ≈ also used in a figurative sense to refer to causing things to happen

[PSA 7:15](https://ref.ly/Ps7:15) · [SNG 8:5](https://ref.ly/Song8:5) · [SNG 8:5](https://ref.ly/Song8:5)

1 MIC 2:10 BDB and KB prefer to read תְּחַבֵּל וְחֶבֶל as תְּחֻבְּלוּ חֶבֶל, which turns the verb into a passive, but doesn't really alter its meaning \| HOTTP prefers to maintain the interpretation of MT. 2 JOB 24:9 MT ESV \| LXX עֻל RSV NIV "infant" NJPS NRSV REB "child" 3 JOB 17:1 Some commentators say that here "spirit" refers to the desire to live rather than to life itself. The immediate context suggests, however, that Job is (at least according to his own observations) about to die \| KB "my spirit is disturbed, which is technically possible, but does not fit the context as well as the interpretation that has been chosen here.

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 22:25; Deuteronomy 24:6; Deuteronomy 24:17; Job 22:6; Job 24:3; Job 24:9; Proverbs 20:16; Proverbs 27:13; Ezekiel 18:16; Amos 2:8; Ezra 6:12; Proverbs 13:13; Ecclesiastes 5:5; Song of Songs 2:15; Isaiah 13:5; Isaiah 32:7; Isaiah 54:16; Daniel 4:20; Daniel 6:23; Micah 2:10; Job 17:1; Isaiah 10:27; Daniel 2:44; Daniel 6:27; Daniel 7:14; Nehemiah 1:7; Job 34:31; Psalms 7:15; Song of Songs 8:5

## חֶבֶל (id: 002090000000000)

חֶבֶל
=====

חֶבֶל (H2256a · H2256d)

noun m · חבל

Cords

rope, cord \= piece of stout cord; ◄ made by twisting together palm fibres, linen, or reeds; ► used for tying and keeping things together, climbing, measuring, drawing things to oneself, making traps, etc.; ≈ often used in a figurative sense to refer to conditions that try to take control of people; a rope tied around the head is a symbol of submission

[JOS 2:15](https://ref.ly/Josh2:15) · [2SA 8:2](https://ref.ly/2Sam8:2) · [2SA 8:2](https://ref.ly/2Sam8:2) · [2SA 8:2](https://ref.ly/2Sam8:2) · [2SA 17:13](https://ref.ly/2Sam17:13) · [1KI 20:31](https://ref.ly/1Kgs20:31) · [1KI 20:32](https://ref.ly/1Kgs20:32) · [EST 1:6](https://ref.ly/Esth1:6) · [JOB 40:25](https://ref.ly/Job40:25) · [PSA 16:6](https://ref.ly/Ps16:6) · [PSA 78:55](https://ref.ly/Ps78:55) · [ECC 12:6](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:6) · [ISA 5:18](https://ref.ly/Isa5:18)1 · [ISA 5:18](https://ref.ly/Isa5:18)1 · [ISA 5:18](https://ref.ly/Isa5:18)1 · [ISA 33:20](https://ref.ly/Isa33:20) · [ISA 33:23](https://ref.ly/Isa33:23) · [JER 38:6](https://ref.ly/Jer38:6) · [JER 38:11](https://ref.ly/Jer38:11) · [JER 38:12](https://ref.ly/Jer38:12) · [JER 38:13](https://ref.ly/Jer38:13) · [EZK 27:24](https://ref.ly/Ezek27:24) · [HOS 11:4](https://ref.ly/Hos11:4) · [AMO 7:17](https://ref.ly/Amos7:17) · [MIC 2:5](https://ref.ly/Mic2:5) · [ZEC 2:5](https://ref.ly/Zech2:5)

Traps

noose, trap literally: rope; hence: \= rope tied into a noose, attached to the other end to a bent bough or small tree that springs upright and tightens the noose around the victim when the trap is sprung; ► used for hunting animals; ≈ associated with aggression and control

[2SA 22:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:6) · [JOB 18:10](https://ref.ly/Job18:10) · [JOB 36:8](https://ref.ly/Job36:8) · [PSA 18:5](https://ref.ly/Ps18:5) · [PSA 18:6](https://ref.ly/Ps18:6) · [PSA 116:3](https://ref.ly/Ps116:3) · [PSA 119:61](https://ref.ly/Ps119:61) · [PSA 140:6](https://ref.ly/Ps140:6) · [PRO 5:22](https://ref.ly/Prov5:22)

Land

area, land, district literally: rope (of land); hence: \= piece of land; ► owned or occupied by an individual or a group of people

[DEU 3:4](https://ref.ly/Deut3:4) · [DEU 3:13](https://ref.ly/Deut3:13) · [DEU 3:14](https://ref.ly/Deut3:14) · [JOS 17:5](https://ref.ly/Josh17:5) · [JOS 17:14](https://ref.ly/Josh17:14) · [JOS 19:9](https://ref.ly/Josh19:9) · [JOS 19:29](https://ref.ly/Josh19:29) · [1KI 4:13](https://ref.ly/1Kgs4:13) · [1CH 16:18](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:18) · [PSA 105:11](https://ref.ly/Ps105:11) · [EZK 47:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek47:13) · [ZEP 2:5](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:5) · [ZEP 2:6](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:6) · [ZEP 2:7](https://ref.ly/Zeph2:7)

Possess

possession, property \= object that is owned by someone else

[DEU 32:9](https://ref.ly/Deut32:9)

Associate

group, band literally: rope (of people); hence: \= a group of people

[1SA 10:5](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:5) · [1SA 10:10](https://ref.ly/1Sam10:10)

noun m · חבל

Impact

destruction \= act of bringing destruction and suffering upon objects

[MIC 2:10](https://ref.ly/Mic2:10)1

1 ISA 5:18 · MIC 2:10 Some commentators suppose that "cord of deceit" refers to the knotted strands of a cord used in a Babylonian magical ritual to attract evil (De Waard 1997:27\).

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Joshua 2:15; 2 Samuel 8:2; 2 Samuel 17:13; 1 Kings 20:31; 1 Kings 20:32; Esther 1:6; Job 40:25; Psalms 16:6; Psalms 78:55; Ecclesiastes 12:6; Isaiah 5:18; Isaiah 33:20; Isaiah 33:23; Jeremiah 38:6; Jeremiah 38:11; Jeremiah 38:12; Jeremiah 38:13; Ezekiel 27:24; Hosea 11:4; Amos 7:17; Micah 2:5; Zechariah 2:5; 2 Samuel 22:6; Job 18:10; Job 36:8; Psalms 18:5; Psalms 18:6; Psalms 116:3; Psalms 119:61; Psalms 140:6; Proverbs 5:22; Deuteronomy 3:4; Deuteronomy 3:13; Deuteronomy 3:14; Joshua 17:5; Joshua 17:14; Joshua 19:9; Joshua 19:29; 1 Kings 4:13; 1 Chronicles 16:18; Psalms 105:11; Ezekiel 47:13; Zephaniah 2:5; Zephaniah 2:6; Zephaniah 2:7; Deuteronomy 32:9; 1 Samuel 10:5; 1 Samuel 10:10; Micah 2:10

## חֲבַצִּנְיָה (id: 002095000000000)

חֲבַצִּנְיָה
============

חֲבַצִּנְיָה (H2262)

name

Dress

to gird \= causative action by which someone ties a belt or piece of cloth around someone else's waist

Dress

**Collocation:** חגר מָתְנַיִם

to gird one's loins, to tuck one's cloak into one's belt, to tie up one's skirts literally: to gird (one's) loins; hence: \= action by which humans pull up their robes and tie a belt or piece of cloth around their waist to keep it in place, ► in order to be able walk or work without being hampered

[2KI 4:29](https://ref.ly/2Kgs4:29) · [2KI 9:1](https://ref.ly/2Kgs9:1)

Strong

**Collocation:** חגר מָתְנַיִם בְּעֹוז

to summon (one's) strength literally: to gird (one's) loins with strength; hence: \= action by which humans rally their physical strength

[PRO 31:17](https://ref.ly/Prov31:17)

verb

Unable

to limp \= action by which someone walks slowly and with difficulty

[2SA 22:46](https://ref.ly/2Sam22:46)2

## חדד (id: 002130000000000)

חדד
===

חדד (H2300)

verb · חַד · חֲדַד · חַדּוּד · חָדִיד

Shape

to sharpen \= causative action by which humans use an iron tool to cause an object to have a thin cutting edge, ► in order to make it useful and effective as a tool; ≈ often associated with aggression and danger

[PRO 27:17](https://ref.ly/Prov27:17) · [EZK 21:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:14) · [EZK 21:15](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:15) · [EZK 21:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:16) · [EZK 21:21](https://ref.ly/Ezek21:21)1

Ferocious

to be fierce, to be dangerous \= state in which animals are inclined to violent and dangerous activity ◄ as dangerous as a sharp knife

[HAB 1:8](https://ref.ly/Hab1:8)

Know

**Collocation:** חדד פָּנִים

to sharpen (someone's) face \> wit literally: to sharpen someone's face; hence: \= causative action by which humans increase the ability of others to assess different situations and react in an effective way

[PRO 27:17](https://ref.ly/Prov27:17)

1 EZK 21:21 RSV REB \| MT HOTTP\-C הִתְאַחֲדִי \= אחד

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Proverbs 27:17; Ezekiel 21:14; Ezekiel 21:15; Ezekiel 21:16; Ezekiel 21:21; Habakkuk 1:8

חדה

## חוּג (id: 002155000000000)

חוּג
====

חוּג (H2329)

noun m

Regions Above the Earth

circle, horizon, vault, dome, canopy \= dome\-shaped structure; used exclusively to denote the firmament, which separates the waters above the earth from the earth itself; ≈ God is said to have his dwelling\-place above this structure; it is also regarded as the boundary between light and darkness

## חוה (id: 002157000000000)

חוה
===

חוה (A0263 · A2324 · H2331 · H7812) — שׁחה

verb · אַחֲוָה

Speak · Know

to tell, to inform, to impart, to show \= causative action by which humans convey information to other humans through speech

[JOB 15:17](https://ref.ly/Job15:17) · [JOB 32:6](https://ref.ly/Job32:6) · [JOB 32:10](https://ref.ly/Job32:10) · [JOB 32:17](https://ref.ly/Job32:17) · [JOB 36:2](https://ref.ly/Job36:2) · [PSA 19:3](https://ref.ly/Ps19:3) · [DAN 2:4](https://ref.ly/Dan2:4) · [DAN 2:6](https://ref.ly/Dan2:6) · [DAN 2:6](https://ref.ly/Dan2:6) · [DAN 2:7](https://ref.ly/Dan2:7) · [DAN 2:9](https://ref.ly/Dan2:9) · [DAN 2:10](https://ref.ly/Dan2:10) · [DAN 2:11](https://ref.ly/Dan2:11) · [DAN 2:16](https://ref.ly/Dan2:16) · [DAN 2:24](https://ref.ly/Dan2:24) · [DAN 2:27](https://ref.ly/Dan2:27) · [DAN 3:32](https://ref.ly/Dan3:32) · [DAN 5:7](https://ref.ly/Dan5:7) · [DAN 5:12](https://ref.ly/Dan5:12) · [DAN 5:12](https://ref.ly/Dan5:12) · [DAN 5:15](https://ref.ly/Dan5:15)

verb

Stance

to bow down, to get down, to fall prostrate \= action by which humans lay themselves flat on the ground

[ISA 51:23](https://ref.ly/Isa51:23)

Bow

to bow down, to worship literally: to bow down; hence: \= action by which humans lay themselves down on the ground in front of another human or a deity, ► as an act of submission or respect

Bear

**Collocation:** חול עַל־רֹאשׁ

to fall on the head (of someone) literally: to turn over someone's head; hence: \= process by which a certain condition become someone's responsibility

Engage

## חזה (id: 002189000000000)

חזה
===

חזה (A2370 · H2372)

## חֵזֶק (id: 002205000000000)

חֵזֶק
=====

חֵזֶק (H2391)

noun m · חזק · חִזְקִי · חִזְקִיָּה · חִזְקִיָּהוּ

Titles

strength literally: (one's) strength; hence: \= a title for God as the one who grants strength to his people

Reinier de Blois

## חָח (id: 002213000000000)

חָח
===

חָח (H2397)

noun m · חֹוחַ

Traps

hook \= small, curved piece of metal or bone or even a strong thorn, with a sharp point on one end, usually with a barb just behind the point, and a loop or bend on the other end to which a line can be attached; ► used to catch and control animals; ≈ associated with aggression and control

[2KI 19:28](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:28) · [ISA 37:29](https://ref.ly/Isa37:29) · [EZK 19:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek19:4) · [EZK 19:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek19:9) · [EZK 29:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:4) · [EZK 38:4](https://ref.ly/Ezek38:4)

Jewellery

brooch, pin \= object with a pin, ◄ made out of metal; ► usually fastened to a woman's dress and functioning as an ornament

[EXO 35:22](https://ref.ly/Exod35:22)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** 2 Kings 19:28; Isaiah 37:29; Ezekiel 19:4; Ezekiel 19:9; Ezekiel 29:4; Ezekiel 38:4; Exodus 35:22


## חטא (id: 002214000000000)

חטא
===

חטא (H2398a)

verb

Move

to withdraw, to draw back \= action by which a human being moves in a backward direction

[JOB 41:17](https://ref.ly/Job41:17)

verb · חֵטְא · חַטָּא · חֲטָאָה · חֶטְאָה · חַטָּאָה · חַטָּאת · חֲטָא

Fail

to fail, to miss, to forfeit \= state in which a human being is unable to succeed in what s/he intend to do

[JDG 20:16](https://ref.ly/Judg20:16) · [JOB 5:24](https://ref.ly/Job5:24) · [PRO 8:36](https://ref.ly/Prov8:36) · [PRO 19:2](https://ref.ly/Prov19:2) · [PRO 20:2](https://ref.ly/Prov20:2) · [ISA 65:20](https://ref.ly/Isa65:20) · [HAB 2:10](https://ref.ly/Hab2:10)

Guilty

to stand guilty, to be at fault, to bear the blame for (a specific sinful action) \= state in which a human being bears the responsibility for a wrongful act against God or someone else, ► which results in a state of guilt which may require atonement, restitution, and retribution

[GEN 43:9](https://ref.ly/Gen43:9) · [GEN 44:32](https://ref.ly/Gen44:32) · [EXO 5:16](https://ref.ly/Exod5:16)

Non\-Possess

to take responsibility, to bear the loss \= action by which a human being takes the responsibility for something that has been killed or destroyed and makes restitution for it

[GEN 31:39](https://ref.ly/Gen31:39)

Guilty

**Collocation:** חטא בָּשָׂר

to bring guilt upon oneself literally: to bring guilt upon (one's) flesh; hence: \= causative action by which a human being commits a wrongful act against God or someone else ► and so brings his/her own body in a state of guilt which may require atonement, restitution, and retribution

[ECC 5:5](https://ref.ly/Eccl5:5)

Guilty

to bring guilt upon, to cause to be declared guilty \= causative action by which a human being brings upon someone else the responsibility for a wrongful act against God or someone else, ► which brings upon that person a state of guilt which may require atonement, restitution, and retribution

[DEU 24:4](https://ref.ly/Deut24:4) · [ISA 29:21](https://ref.ly/Isa29:21)

Sin

to sin, to commit sin \= action by which a human being commits a wrongful act against God or someone else, whether or not on purpose, ► which may require atonement, restitution, and/or retribution

Sin

sinful object, object that leads to sin \= object associated with wrongful acts against God or someone else

[DEU 9:21](https://ref.ly/Deut9:21) · [HOS 10:8](https://ref.ly/Hos10:8)

Chastise

punishment \= process by which a human being receives the treatment that is the consequence of a wrongful act that s/he has committed

[LAM 4:6](https://ref.ly/Lam4:6) · [ZEC 14:19](https://ref.ly/Zech14:19) · [ZEC 14:19](https://ref.ly/Zech14:19)

Clean

cleansing, purification \= causative action by which a human being performs ritual of removing the state of guilt or uncleanness from a person or object

Sacrifice

sin\-offering \= action by which a human being performs the sacrificial ritual that is intended to remove the state of guilt from oneself or someone else

## חטב (id: 002222000000000)

חטב
===

חטב (H2404)

verb

Impact

to cut (down), to carve \= causative action by which humans strike an object repeatedly with an axe, chisel, or a similar sharp tool ► in order to cut it down or alter its shape

[DEU 19:5](https://ref.ly/Deut19:5) · [DEU 29:10](https://ref.ly/Deut29:10) · [JOS 9:21](https://ref.ly/Josh9:21) · [JOS 9:23](https://ref.ly/Josh9:23) · [JOS 9:27](https://ref.ly/Josh9:27) · [2CH 2:9](https://ref.ly/2Chr2:9) · [PSA 144:12](https://ref.ly/Ps144:12) · [JER 46:22](https://ref.ly/Jer46:22) · [EZK 39:10](https://ref.ly/Ezek39:10)

verb

Cloth

multi\-colored meaning unsure; possibly: \= cloth dyed in multiple colors

[PRO 7:16](https://ref.ly/Prov7:16)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 19:5; Deuteronomy 29:10; Joshua 9:21; Joshua 9:23; Joshua 9:27; 2 Chronicles 2:9; Psalms 144:12; Jeremiah 46:22; Ezekiel 39:10; Proverbs 7:16


## חֲטֻבֹות (id: 002223000000000)

חֲטֻבֹות
========

חֲטֻבֹות (H2405)

verb · חטב

Cloth

colored cloth \= cloth dyed with many different colors; ≈ considered beautiful

[PRO 7:16](https://ref.ly/Prov7:16)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Proverbs 7:16


## חִטָּה (id: 002224000000000)

חִטָּה
======

חִטָּה (H2406)

noun f · חנט

Crops

wheat \= cereal plant bearing dense four\-sided spike of grain; ◄ Triticum; ► important source of flour for bread; ≈ its color used to be regarded as the ideal color for the skin

## חיה (id: 002235000000000)

חיה

## חַיָּה (id: 002236000000000)

חַיָּה
======

חַיָּה (H2416c · H2416d)

noun f · חיה

Alive

alive \= state in which someone is alive and well

[EZK 7:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek7:13)

Animals

living creature, wild land animal, beast possibly shortened form of נֶפֶשׁ חַיָּה "living creature": \= animal; ◄ generic, sometimes referring to all animals, sometimes limited to wild land animals only

## חַיִּים (id: 002240000000000)

חַיִּים
=======

noun m · חיה

Relatives

kinsfolk \= group of people, related by kinship

[1SA 18:18](https://ref.ly/1Sam18:18)

Alive

life \= the state of being alive and well; ◄ because of the presence of air to breathe and food to eat; ≈ life is regarded as more than a mere physical condition; in many cases it includes health, strength, and some degree of prosperity

## חַיִּין (id: 002241000000000)

חַיִּין
=======

חַיִּין (A2417b)

noun m · חיה

Alive

life \= the state of being alive and well; ◄ because of the presence of air to breathe and food to eat; ≈ life is regarded as more than a mere physical condition; in many cases it includes health, strength, and some degree of prosperity

Reinier de Blois

## חיל (id: 002242000000000)

חיל
===

חיל (H2342b)

verb · חִיל · חִילָה · חַלְחָלָה

Spasm

to have labor\-pains \= process by which human have painful contractions of the womb, ◄ which is caused by an advanced state of pregnancy ► and results in birth of new offspring; ≈ associated with anguish, trembling, suffering, and fear

[ISA 26:17](https://ref.ly/Isa26:17) · [ISA 54:1](https://ref.ly/Isa54:1) · [ISA 66:7](https://ref.ly/Isa66:7)

Spasm

to cause to give birth \= causative action by which events cause animals to have painful contractions of the womb; ◄ caused by advanced state of pregnancy; ► results in birth of new offspring

[PSA 29:9](https://ref.ly/Ps29:9)1

Afraid

to tremble, to be distressed, to be in anguish \= state in which humans experience strong fear and distress, ◄ compared to the state of mind of a woman in labor; ► often accompanied by physical side\-effects, like writhing, and trembling

[DEU 2:25](https://ref.ly/Deut2:25) · [1CH 16:30](https://ref.ly/1Chr16:30) · [EST 4:4](https://ref.ly/Esth4:4) · [JOB 15:20](https://ref.ly/Job15:20) · [JOB 26:5](https://ref.ly/Job26:5) · [PSA 55:5](https://ref.ly/Ps55:5) · [PSA 77:17](https://ref.ly/Ps77:17) · [PSA 96:9](https://ref.ly/Ps96:9) · [PSA 97:4](https://ref.ly/Ps97:4) · [PSA 114:7](https://ref.ly/Ps114:7) · [ISA 13:8](https://ref.ly/Isa13:8) · [ISA 23:5](https://ref.ly/Isa23:5) · [ISA 26:18](https://ref.ly/Isa26:18) · [JER 5:3](https://ref.ly/Jer5:3) · [JER 5:22](https://ref.ly/Jer5:22) · [JER 51:29](https://ref.ly/Jer51:29) · [EZK 30:16](https://ref.ly/Ezek30:16) · [JOL 2:6](https://ref.ly/Joel2:6) · [MIC 4:10](https://ref.ly/Mic4:10) · [HAB 3:10](https://ref.ly/Hab3:10) · [ZEC 9:5](https://ref.ly/Zech9:5)

Impact

to be badly wounded \= process by which humans are inflicted with severe wounds so that they writhe in pain and their life is in danger

[1SA 31:3](https://ref.ly/1Sam31:3) · [1CH 10:3](https://ref.ly/1Chr10:3)

Unsteady

to cause to tremble \= causative action by which nature is made to shake and convulse ◄ as if it were a woman in labor

[PSA 29:8](https://ref.ly/Ps29:8) · [PSA 29:8](https://ref.ly/Ps29:8) · [PSA 29:9](https://ref.ly/Ps29:9)1

Birth

to give birth, to bring forth \= process by which humans and animals bring forth new offspring

[DEU 32:18](https://ref.ly/Deut32:18) · [JOB 15:7](https://ref.ly/Job15:7) · [JOB 39:1](https://ref.ly/Job39:1) · [PSA 51:7](https://ref.ly/Ps51:7) · [PRO 8:24](https://ref.ly/Prov8:24) · [PRO 8:25](https://ref.ly/Prov8:25)4 · [ISA 23:4](https://ref.ly/Isa23:4) · [ISA 45:10](https://ref.ly/Isa45:10) · [ISA 51:2](https://ref.ly/Isa51:2) · [ISA 66:8](https://ref.ly/Isa66:8) · [ISA 66:8](https://ref.ly/Isa66:8)

Exist

to bring forth, to create literally: to give birth to objects; hence: \= causative action by which deities bring objects are into existence

[PSA 90:2](https://ref.ly/Ps90:2)5

Happen

to cause, to bring forth literally: to give birth to an event; hence: \= causative process by which events are caused to happen

[PRO 25:23](https://ref.ly/Prov25:23)

verb · חַיִל

Endure

to endure, to linger \= process by which a condition lasts for a relatively long time

[JOB 20:21](https://ref.ly/Job20:21) · [PSA 10:5](https://ref.ly/Ps10:5)

Non\-Engage

to wait \= action by which someone defers action for a specified time or until some expected event occurs

## חֵיל (id: 002244000000000)

====

noun m · חול

Fortifications

outer wall, outer fortification meaning unsure; probably: \= a structure surrounding a town, outside the main wall; ◄ made out of of stones or bricks; ► provides strength and security to the town; ≈ sometimes used metaphorically to denote someone who offers protection

## חֵיק (id: 002254000000000)

חֵיק
====

חֵיק (H2436)

noun m

People

bosom, chest, lap \= front of the body of a human being, which, when a person is sitting down, forms a kind of platform that can be used for activities like throwing the lot, and that can even function as a sitting place for someone else, like a pet animal, a child or a beloved one; ≈ symbolizes affection and intimacy, and sometimes represents the entire person

[GEN 16:5](https://ref.ly/Gen16:5) · [NUM 11:12](https://ref.ly/Num11:12) · [DEU 13:7](https://ref.ly/Deut13:7) · [DEU 28:54](https://ref.ly/Deut28:54) · [DEU 28:56](https://ref.ly/Deut28:56) · [RUT 4:16](https://ref.ly/Ruth4:16) · [2SA 12:3](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:3) · [2SA 12:8](https://ref.ly/2Sam12:8) · [1KI 1:2](https://ref.ly/1Kgs1:2) · [1KI 3:20](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:20) · [1KI 3:20](https://ref.ly/1Kgs3:20) · [1KI 17:19](https://ref.ly/1Kgs17:19) · [JOB 19:27](https://ref.ly/Job19:27) · [PRO 5:20](https://ref.ly/Prov5:20) · [PRO 6:27](https://ref.ly/Prov6:27) · [PRO 16:33](https://ref.ly/Prov16:33) · [ISA 40:11](https://ref.ly/Isa40:11) · [LAM 2:12](https://ref.ly/Lam2:12) · [MIC 7:5](https://ref.ly/Mic7:5)

Chastise

**Collocation:** מדד עַל־חֵיק

חֵךְ
====

חֵךְ (H2441)

noun m · חנך

palate \= upper part of mouth cavity; ◄ part of human body

[JOB 29:10](https://ref.ly/Job29:10) · [PSA 137:6](https://ref.ly/Ps137:6) · [LAM 4:4](https://ref.ly/Lam4:4) · [EZK 3:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek3:26)

mouth \= mouth cavity; ◄ part of human body; ► plays an important role in actions like speaking, blowing, kissing, biting, tasting, and chewing

[JOB 6:30](https://ref.ly/Job6:30) · [JOB 12:11](https://ref.ly/Job12:11) · [JOB 20:13](https://ref.ly/Job20:13) · [JOB 31:30](https://ref.ly/Job31:30) · [JOB 33:2](https://ref.ly/Job33:2) · [JOB 34:3](https://ref.ly/Job34:3) · [PRO 8:7](https://ref.ly/Prov8:7) · [HOS 8:1](https://ref.ly/Hos8:1)

Speak

mouth \> speech, words \= action by which humans utter words; ≈ associated with the palate

[PRO 5:3](https://ref.ly/Prov5:3) · [SNG 5:16](https://ref.ly/Song5:16)1 · [SNG 7:10](https://ref.ly/Song7:10)2

Taste

taste \= process by which humans discover the flavor of food; ≈ associated with the palate

[PRO 24:13](https://ref.ly/Prov24:13) · [SNG 2:3](https://ref.ly/Song2:3)

Know

taste \> evaluation (of someone's words) literally: process of discovering the flavor of an event; hence: \= process by which humans come to a better understanding and evaluation of a certain event

[PSA 119:103](https://ref.ly/Ps119:103)

Impact

mouth \> kissing, kisses \= action by which humans press their lips on someone else's lips or any other part of that person's body

[SNG 5:16](https://ref.ly/Song5:16)1 · [SNG 7:10](https://ref.ly/Song7:10)2

1 SNG 5:16 RSV NJB NRSV \[c] \| GNT CEV \[f] \| NIV NJPS REB allow for both interpretations 2 SNG 7:10 RSV NRSV CEV \[c] \| NIV NJPS NJB REB GNT allow for both \[c] and \[f]

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 29:10; Psalms 137:6; Lamentations 4:4; Ezekiel 3:26; Job 6:30; Job 12:11; Job 20:13; Job 31:30; Job 33:2; Job 34:3; Proverbs 8:7; Hosea 8:1; Proverbs 5:3; Song of Songs 5:16; Song of Songs 7:10; Proverbs 24:13; Song of Songs 2:3; Psalms 119:103


## חכה (id: 002259000000000)

חכה
===

חכה (H2442)

verb · חֲכַלְיָה

to defer action, to wait, to lie in wait, to delay, to hesitate, to long \= action by which humans or deities consciously remain in a particular state

## חכם (id: 002266000000000)

חכם
===

חכם (H2449)

verb · חָכָם · חָכְמָה · חַכִּים · חַכְמֹונִי · תַּחְכְּמֹנִי

Wise

to be able, to be skillful, to be wise, to be intelligent \= state or process by which humans, deities, and animals possess or gain a certain level of wisdom, intelligence, or proficiency

[DEU 32:29](https://ref.ly/Deut32:29) · [1KI 5:11](https://ref.ly/1Kgs5:11) · [JOB 32:9](https://ref.ly/Job32:9) · [PSA 58:6](https://ref.ly/Ps58:6) · [PRO 6:6](https://ref.ly/Prov6:6) · [PRO 8:33](https://ref.ly/Prov8:33) · [PRO 9:9](https://ref.ly/Prov9:9) · [PRO 9:12](https://ref.ly/Prov9:12) · [PRO 9:12](https://ref.ly/Prov9:12) · [PRO 13:20](https://ref.ly/Prov13:20) · [PRO 19:20](https://ref.ly/Prov19:20) · [PRO 20:1](https://ref.ly/Prov20:1) · [PRO 21:11](https://ref.ly/Prov21:11) · [PRO 23:15](https://ref.ly/Prov23:15) · [PRO 23:19](https://ref.ly/Prov23:19) · [PRO 27:11](https://ref.ly/Prov27:11) · [PRO 30:24](https://ref.ly/Prov30:24) · [ECC 2:15](https://ref.ly/Eccl2:15) · [ECC 2:19](https://ref.ly/Eccl2:19) · [ECC 7:23](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:23) · [ZEC 9:2](https://ref.ly/Zech9:2)

Wise

to act wisely \= action by which humans act in accordance to a certain level of wisdom, intelligence, or proficiency

[EXO 1:10](https://ref.ly/Exod1:10) · [ECC 7:16](https://ref.ly/Eccl7:16)

Wise

to teach, to instruct, to make wise \= causative action by which humans or deities cause (other) humans to possess or gain a certain level of wisdom, intelligence, or proficiency

[JOB 35:11](https://ref.ly/Job35:11) · [PSA 19:8](https://ref.ly/Ps19:8) · [PSA 105:22](https://ref.ly/Ps105:22) · [PSA 119:98](https://ref.ly/Ps119:98)

## חָכְמָה (id: 002268000000000)

חָכְמָה
=======

## חָלָב (id: 002274000000000)

חָלָב
=====

חָלָב (H2461)

noun m · חֵלֶב · חֶלְבְּנָה · חֵלֶב

Liquids · Dairy

milk \= white fluid; ◄ secreted by women and female mammals; ► for nourishment of their children or young; also used as food for humans; ≈ highly appreciated and considered high quality food; associated with delight, whiteness, purity, wealth, and well\-being; metaphor for beauty, young age; quality, wealth, and sex

[PSA 19:7](https://ref.ly/Ps19:7)

Celestial Bodies

sun literally: the hot one; hence: \= the heavenly body from which the earth derives its light and warmth; ≈ associated with light and, by extension, with happiness

## חמס (id: 002360000000000)

חמס
===

חמס (H2554)

verb · חָמָס

Ferocious

to harm, to wrong, to mistreat, to abuse \= action by which humans behave aggressively towards other humans with which they have a relationship; ► usually in order to enrich themselves in one way or another

[JOB 21:27](https://ref.ly/Job21:27) · [PRO 8:36](https://ref.ly/Prov8:36) · [JER 13:22](https://ref.ly/Jer13:22) · [JER 22:3](https://ref.ly/Jer22:3) · [EZK 22:26](https://ref.ly/Ezek22:26) · [ZEP 3:4](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:4)

verb

Non\-Whole

to let go, to shed, to drop \= process by which a plant lets go of its fruits

[JOB 15:33](https://ref.ly/Job15:33)

Dissociate

to drop, to let go, to give up \= action by which deities detach themselves from an object to which they used to feel attached

[LAM 2:6](https://ref.ly/Lam2:6)1

1 LAM 2:6 Most translations interpret חמס here as referring to physical destruction of an object. Yet this verb never really has this meaning. The meaning "to drop, let go", however, has been attested, so it not implausible for this verb to have this meaning in this verse as well.

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Job 21:27; Proverbs 8:36; Jeremiah 13:22; Jeremiah 22:3; Ezekiel 22:26; Zephaniah 3:4; Job 15:33; Lamentations 2:6

## חֲמַר (id: 002367000000000)

חֲמַר
=====

חֲמַר (A2562)

noun m

Liquids · Wine · Crops

wine \= dark red alcoholic liquid; ◄ made out of grapes through the process of fermentation; ► used as beverage, though to be avoided by Nazirites, and by priests when on duty; ≈ associated with joy and well\-being, but also with drunkenness and foolishness

[EZR 6:9](https://ref.ly/Ezra6:9) · [EZR 7:22](https://ref.ly/Ezra7:22) · [DAN 5:1](https://ref.ly/Dan5:1) · [DAN 5:2](https://ref.ly/Dan5:2) · [DAN 5:4](https://ref.ly/Dan5:4) · [DAN 5:23](https://ref.ly/Dan5:23)

* **Associated Passages:** Ezra 6:9; Ezra 7:22; Daniel 5:1; Daniel 5:2; Daniel 5:4; Daniel 5:23


## חֵמָר (id: 002368000000000)

חֵמָר
=====

חֵמָר (H2564)

noun m · חמר

Paint

bitumen, tar \= tarlike substance; ◄ naturally derived from petroleum; ► used in certain areas for binding together stones or bricks; also used to make objects watertight

[GEN 11:3](https://ref.ly/Gen11:3) · [GEN 14:10](https://ref.ly/Gen14:10) · [EXO 2:3](https://ref.ly/Exod2:3)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 11:3; Genesis 14:10; Exodus 2:3


## חֶמֶר (id: 002369000000000)

חֶמֶר
=====

חֶמֶר (H2561)

noun m · חמר

Liquids · Wine

(fermenting) wine \= dark red alcoholic liquid in the middle of the fermentation stage; ◄ made out of pressed grapes; ► used as beverage; ≈ associated with well\-being

[DEU 32:14](https://ref.ly/Deut32:14)

1 NEW NOTE en

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Deuteronomy 32:14


## חֹמֶר (id: 002370000000000)

חֹמֶר
=====

חֹמֶר (H2563 · H2565)

noun m · חמר

Dust

mud, clay, mortar \= stiff tenacious earth; ► material of which bricks, pottery, and even man himself is made; ≈ buildings made with this material are regarded as relatively weak as opposed to buildings made of stone; therefore it is also seen as relatively worthless material

[GEN 11:3](https://ref.ly/Gen11:3) · [EXO 1:14](https://ref.ly/Exod1:14) · [JOB 10:9](https://ref.ly/Job10:9) · [JOB 13:12](https://ref.ly/Job13:12) · [JOB 27:16](https://ref.ly/Job27:16) · [JOB 30:19](https://ref.ly/Job30:19) · [JOB 33:6](https://ref.ly/Job33:6) · [JOB 38:14](https://ref.ly/Job38:14) · [ISA 10:6](https://ref.ly/Isa10:6) · [ISA 29:16](https://ref.ly/Isa29:16) · [ISA 41:25](https://ref.ly/Isa41:25) · [ISA 45:9](https://ref.ly/Isa45:9) · [ISA 64:7](https://ref.ly/Isa64:7) · [JER 18:4](https://ref.ly/Jer18:4) · [JER 18:6](https://ref.ly/Jer18:6) · [NAM 3:14](https://ref.ly/Nah3:14)

Weak

**Collocation:** שׁכן בָּתֵּי חֹמֶר

to dwell in houses of clay \> to be a mortal human being literally: to dwell in houses of clay; hence: \= state of being a mortal human being, living in a body that is bound to return to dust one day

[JOB 4:19](https://ref.ly/Job4:19)

noun m · חמר

Capacity

homer \= unit of measure of 220 liters or 6 bushels; equals 10 ephah and 100 omer

[LEV 27:16](https://ref.ly/Lev27:16) · [NUM 11:32](https://ref.ly/Num11:32) · [ISA 5:10](https://ref.ly/Isa5:10) · [EZK 45:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:11) · [EZK 45:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:11) · [EZK 45:11](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:11) · [EZK 45:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:13) · [EZK 45:13](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:13) · [EZK 45:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:14) · [EZK 45:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek45:14) · [HOS 3:2](https://ref.ly/Hos3:2)

noun m · חמר

Unsteady

foaming \= process by which liquids form small bubbles, ◄ due to fermentation

[HAB 3:15](https://ref.ly/Hab3:15)

noun m

Quantity

heap, pile \= quantity of objects lying one on another

[EXO 8:10](https://ref.ly/Exod8:10) · [EXO 8:10](https://ref.ly/Exod8:10) · [JDG 15:16](https://ref.ly/Judg15:16) · [JDG 15:16](https://ref.ly/Judg15:16)

## חמשׁ (id: 002372000000000)

חמשׁ
====

חמשׁ (H2567 · H2571)

verb · חָמֵשׁ

Non\-Whole

to be in battle array meaning unsure; possibly: \= action by which groups of humans divide themselves into five groups ► in order to be able to defend themselves effectively against the enemy

[EXO 13:18](https://ref.ly/Exod13:18) · [JOS 1:14](https://ref.ly/Josh1:14) · [JOS 4:12](https://ref.ly/Josh4:12) · [JDG 7:11](https://ref.ly/Judg7:11)

Non\-Whole

to take the fifth part \= causative action by which humans divide an object into five parts and take one part

[GEN 41:34](https://ref.ly/Gen41:34)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Exodus 13:18; Joshua 1:14; Joshua 4:12; Judges 7:11; Genesis 41:34

## חֹמֶשׁ (id: 002374000000000)

חֹמֶשׁ
======

חֹמֶשׁ (H2569 · H2570)

noun m · חָמֵשׁ

Non\-Whole

fifth part \= fifth part of a certain quantity

[GEN 47:26](https://ref.ly/Gen47:26)

noun m

belly, stomach \= area located below diaphragm, containing stomach and bowels and other contents

[2SA 2:23](https://ref.ly/2Sam2:23) · [2SA 3:27](https://ref.ly/2Sam3:27) · [2SA 4:6](https://ref.ly/2Sam4:6) · [2SA 20:10](https://ref.ly/2Sam20:10)

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 47:26; 2 Samuel 2:23; 2 Samuel 3:27; 2 Samuel 4:6; 2 Samuel 20:10


## חֲמָת (id: 002375000000000)

חֲמָת
=====

חֲמָת (H2574 · H2578 · H2579) — חֲמָת צֹובָא, חֲמָת צֹובָה, חֲמָת רַבָּה

name · חֲמָתִי

Names of Locations

Hamath \= town, area; ◄ on Orontes river in Syria; ► capital of Aramean kingdom; its inhabitants were relocated to Samaria by the king of Assyria

name

## חֲסִידָה (id: 002420000000000)

חֲסִידָה
========

חֲסִידָה (H2624)

noun f · חסד

Birds

stork \= large bird with long legs and a long neck; the white stork has a white body and black wings, whereas the black stork is a glossy brownish black color with a white belly; both varieties have a red beak and legs; both types spend most of the time on the ground or in shallow water searching for food; the white stork eats mainly locusts, grasshoppers, and other insects, as well as frogs, lizards, and the chicks of ground\-nesting birds, whereas the black stork prefers fish and frogs but also eats the same things as the white stork; ◄ \|iCiconia ciconia\|i\* or \|iCiconia nigra\|i\*; ► unclean and therefore not to be eaten

[LEV 11:19](https://ref.ly/Lev11:19) · [DEU 14:18](https://ref.ly/Deut14:18) · [JOB 39:13](https://ref.ly/Job39:13)1 · [PSA 104:17](https://ref.ly/Ps104:17) · [JER 8:7](https://ref.ly/Jer8:7) · [ZEC 5:9](https://ref.ly/Zech5:9)

noun f · חסד

Love

love \= state of having affection for other animate objects and be willing to care of them

[JOB 39:13](https://ref.ly/Job39:13)1

1 JOB 39:13 HOTTP\-B RSV \[2] \| NIV NJB NJPS GNT CEV \[1] \| NRSV REB חסר "to lack (plumage), be stunted"

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Leviticus 11:19; Deuteronomy 14:18; Job 39:13; Psalms 104:17; Jeremiah 8:7; Zechariah 5:9

noun f · חפר

Animals

mole rat meaning unsure; possibly: \= gray rodent, that grows to about twenty centimeters in length, with very large teeth that protrude from the front of the mouth; they live almost entirely underground, digging their tunnels just below the ground surface with their large teeth and flat front paws; from time to time they eject surplus soil onto the surface of the ground, making small heaps, and thereby giving away their presence; they are blind, and live on roots.

arrow \= pointed missile, shot from a bow; slender and straight in shape and moving swiftly; ◄ made out of wood and/or iron; ► mainly used for hunting, in warfare, and occasionally for divination; ≈ symbol of aggression, affliction, and punishment

Weapons

bow literally: arrow, but used metonymically; hence: \= a strong but flexible piece of wood to which a string is attached for the firing of arrows, ► used for hunting or as weapon of war

arrow \> lightning literally: arrow; hence: \= visible electric discharge between cloud and ground, shaped and moving like an arrow and considered to consist of fire

1 JDG 5:11 \-HOTTP\-A MT KB CEV \| BDB NJPS "archers" \| RSV NRSV "musicians" \| NIV "singers" \| NJB "shepherds" \| REB "merrymakers" \| GNT "noisy crowds" 2 JOB 21:21 This passage is somewhat obscure. Most translations have translated this occurrence of חצץ as "to cut off, which may fit the context well. Nevertheless the interpretation chosen here is closer to the way this verb is used in other passages.

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Proverbs 30:27; Judges 5:11; Job 21:21

## חקק (id: 002501000000000)

חקק
===

חקק (H2710)

verb · חוּקֹק · חֹק · חקה · חֻקָּה

Write

to carve, to portray, to draw, to mark out, to write \= action by which humans reproduce the form or shape of an object on another object; ◄ by carving, drawing, writing, etc.; ► for the purpose of decoration, communication, sometimes as preparation for a new construction

[JOB 19:23](https://ref.ly/Job19:23) · [PRO 8:27](https://ref.ly/Prov8:27) · [PRO 8:29](https://ref.ly/Prov8:29) · [ISA 30:8](https://ref.ly/Isa30:8) · [ISA 49:16](https://ref.ly/Isa49:16) · [EZK 4:1](https://ref.ly/Ezek4:1) · [EZK 23:14](https://ref.ly/Ezek23:14)

Exist

to hew out \= to construct by making cuts in stone

[ISA 22:16](https://ref.ly/Isa22:16)

Happen

to decree, to issue (a decree) \= causative action by which humans prescribe patterns of behavior required from other humans under their authority

[PRO 8:15](https://ref.ly/Prov8:15) · [PRO 31:5](https://ref.ly/Prov31:5) · [ISA 10:1](https://ref.ly/Isa10:1)

Leaders

commander, leader literally: one who decrees; hence: \= person who is in a position of authority over other people

[DEU 33:21](https://ref.ly/Deut33:21) · [JDG 5:9](https://ref.ly/Judg5:9) · [JDG 5:14](https://ref.ly/Judg5:14) · [ISA 33:22](https://ref.ly/Isa33:22)

Tools

sceptre, ruler's staff \= object shaped in such a way that it can be held in one's hand; ◄ usually made out of wood and/or metal; ► held by people in authority, like kings; ≈ symbolizes the position of authority of the person holding it

[GEN 49:10](https://ref.ly/Gen49:10) · [NUM 21:18](https://ref.ly/Num21:18) · [PSA 108:9](https://ref.ly/Ps108:9) · [PSA 60:9](https://ref.ly/Ps60:9)

## חרב (id: 002507000000000)

חרב
===

חרב (H2717 · A2718)

verb · חָרֵב · חֹרֶב · חָרָבָה · חָרְבָּה · חֲרָבֹון · חֹרֵב

Dry

to become dry, to dry up \= process by which a body of water or place that was formerly covered with moisture dries up, ◄ as a result of evaporation or draining; ► in the case of land, if this condition persists, sedentary life will become impossible

[GEN 8:13](https://ref.ly/Gen8:13) · [GEN 8:13](https://ref.ly/Gen8:13) · [JOB 14:11](https://ref.ly/Job14:11) · [PSA 106:9](https://ref.ly/Ps106:9) · [ISA 19:5](https://ref.ly/Isa19:5) · [ISA 19:6](https://ref.ly/Isa19:6) · [ISA 44:27](https://ref.ly/Isa44:27) · [HOS 13:15](https://ref.ly/Hos13:15)

Dry

to dry, to make dry, to cause to dry up \= causative action by which humans or deities cause a state of dryness; ► in the case of land, if this condition persists, sedentary life will become impossible

[JDG 16:7](https://ref.ly/Judg16:7) · [JDG 16:8](https://ref.ly/Judg16:8) · [2KI 19:24](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:24) · [ISA 37:25](https://ref.ly/Isa37:25) · [ISA 42:15](https://ref.ly/Isa42:15) · [ISA 50:2](https://ref.ly/Isa50:2) · [ISA 51:10](https://ref.ly/Isa51:10) · [JER 51:36](https://ref.ly/Jer51:36) · [NAM 1:4](https://ref.ly/Nah1:4)

Impact

to be destroyed, to lie in ruins \= state in which land, constructions, or towns have been totally of destroyed, including the people living there, to the extent that sedentary life is no more possible there

[EZR 4:15](https://ref.ly/Ezra4:15) · [ISA 34:10](https://ref.ly/Isa34:10) · [ISA 60:12](https://ref.ly/Isa60:12) · [ISA 60:12](https://ref.ly/Isa60:12) · [JER 2:12](https://ref.ly/Jer2:12) · [JER 26:9](https://ref.ly/Jer26:9) · [EZK 6:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:6) · [EZK 6:6](https://ref.ly/Ezek6:6) · [EZK 12:20](https://ref.ly/Ezek12:20) · [EZK 26:19](https://ref.ly/Ezek26:19) · [EZK 30:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek30:7) · [AMO 7:9](https://ref.ly/Amos7:9)

Impact

to destroy, to lay waste, to cause destruction \= causative action by which humans and deities cause total destruction to lands, constructions, or towns, including the people living there, either directly or through the hands of others, to the extent that sedentary life is no more possible there

[JDG 16:24](https://ref.ly/Judg16:24) · [2KI 19:17](https://ref.ly/2Kgs19:17) · [ISA 37:18](https://ref.ly/Isa37:18) · [ISA 49:17](https://ref.ly/Isa49:17) · [EZK 19:7](https://ref.ly/Ezek19:7) · [EZK 26:2](https://ref.ly/Ezek26:2) · [EZK 29:12](https://ref.ly/Ezek29:12) · [ZEP 3:6](https://ref.ly/Zeph3:6)

verb · חֶרֶב

Dead

to fight, to kill, to put to the sword \= causative action by which humans fight each other with a sword, usually resulting in death

[2KI 3:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:23)1 · [2KI 3:23](https://ref.ly/2Kgs3:23) · [JER 50:21](https://ref.ly/Jer50:21) · [JER 50:27](https://ref.ly/Jer50:27)

1 2KI 3:23 This is a combination of a hoph. infinitive with a niph. perfect \| BDB KB mention the possibility of revocalizing הָחֳרֵב as הֵחָרֵב so that both forms will be in the niph.

Reinier de Blois

* **Associated Passages:** Genesis 8:13; Job 14:11; Psalms 106:9; Isaiah 19:5; Isaiah 19:6; Isaiah 44:27; Hosea 13:15; Judges 16:7; Judges 16:8; 2 Kings 19:24; Isaiah 37:25; Isaiah 42:15; Isaiah 50:2; Isaiah 51:10; Jeremiah 51:36; Nahum 1:4; Ezra 4:15; Isaiah 34:10; Isaiah 60:12; Jeremiah 2:12; Jeremiah 26:9; Ezekiel 6:6; Ezekiel 12:20; Ezekiel 26:19; Ezekiel 30:7; Amos 7:9; Judges 16:24; 2 Kings 19:17; Isaiah 37:18; Isaiah 49:17; Ezekiel 19:7; Ezekiel 26:2; Ezekiel 29:12; Zephaniah 3:6; 2 Kings 3:23; Jeremiah 50:21; Jeremiah 50:27

Weapons

battering\-ram \= a long, heavy object, ◄ made of wood and covered on one end with metal, ► rammed by soldiers against the wall or gate of a city under siege; it sometimes had a point since the purpose of the ramming was to wedge a hole in the wall; others were blunt on the end; it could be held and swung by soldiers, or sometimes it was suspended by ropes from a moveable wooden tower

[EZK 26:9](https://ref.ly/Ezek26:9)

Conflict

sword \> war \= action by which humans are engaged in an armed conflict with other humans, accompanied by deeds of aggression

Impact

Impact

Unwilling

**Collocation:** לֹא חשׂךְ רֹק

## חשׁך (id: 002599000000000)

חשׁך
====

חשׁך (H2821)

verb · חָשֹׁךְ · חֹשֶׁךְ · חֲשֵׁכָה · מַחְשָׁךְ

Dark

to grow dark, to be darkened \= process by which the light gradually disappears, ◄ caused by the fact that the light of sun, moon, and stars can no longer reach the location that is in focus, ► resulting in a state in which no one can readily see, and colors and shapes can no longer be distinguished; loved by the wicked only; ≈ associated with hardship, death, and lack of enlightenment

Dark

to bring darkness, to make dark, to darken \= causative process by which deities cause the light to gradually disappear, ◄ by making sure that the light of sun, moon, and stars can no longer reach the location that is in focus, ► resulting in a state in which no one can readily see, and colors and shapes can no longer be distinguished; loved by the wicked only; ≈ associated with hardship

[PSA 105:28](https://ref.ly/Ps105:28) · [JER 13:16](https://ref.ly/Jer13:16) · [AMO 5:8](https://ref.ly/Amos5:8) · [AMO 8:9](https://ref.ly/Amos8:9)

Color

[EXO 10:15](https://ref.ly/Exod10:15) · [LAM 4:8](https://ref.ly/Lam4:8)

See

to grow dim literally: eyes are darkened; hence: \= state in which the human eye can no longer see very well

[PSA 69:24](https://ref.ly/Ps69:24) · [ECC 12:3](https://ref.ly/Eccl12:3) · [LAM 5:17](https://ref.ly/Lam5:17)

Foolish

to obscure \= causative action by which humans cause an event to appear void of wisdom or understanding

Know
